\begin{document}
\maketitle

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\KeywordTok{data}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"montgomery.subset"}\NormalTok{)}
\KeywordTok{data}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"uCovar"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{next-generation-sequencing-differential-expression}{%
\section{1. Next Generation Sequencing: Differential
Expression}\label{next-generation-sequencing-differential-expression}}

\hypertarget{a-calculate-rpkm}{%
\subsection{a) Calculate RPKM}\label{a-calculate-rpkm}}

RPKM stands for reads per kilobases per million reads and is calculated
by
\(\frac{r_g}{l_g T}=\frac{\text{# of mapped reads}}{\text{length in Kb}*\text{total mapped reads in millions}}\):

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{lg =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{uCovar}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{length }\OperatorTok{/}\StringTok{ }\DecValTok{1000}
\NormalTok{t =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{unlist}\NormalTok{(montgomery.subset))}
\NormalTok{rpkm =}\StringTok{ }\NormalTok{montgomery.subset}\OperatorTok{/}\NormalTok{(lg}\OperatorTok{*}\NormalTok{t)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Do a standard t test between the groups for each gene:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{# T test for each row}
\NormalTok{t_tests =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{apply}\NormalTok{(rpkm,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(x)\{}
\NormalTok{  group1 =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(x[}\DecValTok{1}\OperatorTok{:}\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{  group2 =}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(x[}\DecValTok{6}\OperatorTok{:}\DecValTok{10}\NormalTok{])}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{var}\NormalTok{(group1)}\OperatorTok{==}\DecValTok{0} \OperatorTok{|}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{var}\NormalTok{(group2)}\OperatorTok{==}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)\{ }\CommentTok{# Skip those with constant values }
\NormalTok{    t}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic=}\OtherTok{NA}
\NormalTok{    t}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value=}\OtherTok{NA}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{    t <-}\StringTok{ }\KeywordTok{t.test}\NormalTok{(group1,group2)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \KeywordTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\KeywordTok{c}\NormalTok{(t}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic,t}\OperatorTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value))}
\NormalTok{\})}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
